\chapter{Change Log}
\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG}{}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG}\index{Change Log@{Change Log}}
\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9317}%
\Hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9317}%
 All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file. This project adheres to \href{http://semver.org/}{\texttt{ Semantic Versioning}}.

This change log follows the format documented in \href{http://keepachangelog.com/}{\texttt{ Keep a CHANGELOG}}.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9318}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v4.\+1.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/09-\/17}{v4.\+1.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/09-\/17}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9318}
This release adds time zone support to format functions (that I somehow missed when working on the feature) and fixes a few bugs.

Make sure also upgrade {\ttfamily TZDate} to v1.\+0.\+2 as it \href{https://github.com/date-fns/tz/blob/main/CHANGELOG.md\#v102---2024-09-14}{\texttt{ includes a bunch of critical bug fixes}}.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9319}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9319}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed internal {\ttfamily construct\+From} throwing an exception on {\ttfamily null} arguments. While {\ttfamily null} isn\textquotesingle{}t allowed, the functions should rather return {\ttfamily Invalid Date} or {\ttfamily NaN} in such cases. See \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/3885}{\texttt{ \#3885}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9320}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9320}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added missing time zone support to {\ttfamily format}, {\ttfamily format\+ISO}, {\ttfamily format\+ISO9075}, {\ttfamily format\+Relative} and {\ttfamily format\+RFC3339}. See \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/3886}{\texttt{ \#3886}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9321}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v4.\+0.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/09-\/16}{v4.\+0.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/09-\/16}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9321}
I have great news! First, ten years after its release, date-\/fns finally gets first-\/class time zone support.

Another great news is that there aren\textquotesingle{}t many breaking changes in this release. All of them are type-\/related and will affect only those explicitly using internal date-\/fns types. Finally, it has been less than a year since the last major release, which is an improvement over the previous four years between v2 and v3. I plan on keeping the pace and minimizing breaking changes moving forward.

\href{https://blog.date-fns.org/v40-with-time-zone-support/}{\texttt{ Read more about the release in the announcement blog post}}.

-\/ \href{https://twitter.com/kossnocorp}{\texttt{ Sasha @kossnocorp}}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9322}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9322}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added time zones support via \href{https://github.com/date-fns/tz}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily @date-\/fns/tz}}}\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily TZDate} class and {\ttfamily tz} helper function. See its \href{https://github.com/date-fns/tz}{\texttt{ README}} for the details about the API.
\item All relevant functions now accept the context {\ttfamily in} option, which allows to specify the time zone to make the calculations in. If the function also returns a date, it will be in the specified time zone\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ addDays,\ startOfDay\ \}\ from\ "{}date-\/fns"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ tz\ \}\ from\ "{}@date-\/fns/tz"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{startOfDay(addDays(Date.now(),\ 5,\ \{\ in:\ tz("{}Asia/Singapore"{})\ \}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{//=>\ "{}2024-\/09-\/16T00:00:00.000+08:00"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


In the example, {\ttfamily add\+Days} will get the current date and time in Singapore and add 5 days to it. {\ttfamily start\+Of\+Day} will inherit the date type and return the start of the day in Singapore.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9323}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9323}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The function arguments, as well as {\ttfamily Interval}\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily start} and {\ttfamily end}, now can be of different types, allowing you to mix {\ttfamily UTCDate}, {\ttfamily TZDate}, {\ttfamily Date}, and other extensions, as well as primitives (strings and numbers).

The functions will normalize these values, make calculations, and return the result in the same type, preventing any bugs caused by the discrepancy. If passed, the type will be inferred from the context {\ttfamily in} option or the first encountered argument object type. The {\ttfamily Interval}\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily start} and {\ttfamily end} will be considered separately, starting from {\ttfamily start}.

In the given example, the result will be in the {\ttfamily TZDate} as the first argument is a number, and the {\ttfamily start} takes precedence over the {\ttfamily end}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{clamp(Date.now(),\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ start:\ new\ TZDate(start,\ "{}Asia/Singapore"{}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ end:\ new\ UTCDate(),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//=>\ TZDate}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: This release contains a bunch of types changes that should not affect the library\textquotesingle{}s expected usage. The changes are primarily internal and nuanced, so rather than listing them here, I recommend you running the type checker after the upgrade. If there are unfixable problems, please \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/new}{\texttt{ open an issue}}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: The package now is ESM-\/first. The Common\+JS is still support and It should not affect most users, but it might break in certains environments. If you encounter any issues, please \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/new}{\texttt{ report them}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9324}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9324}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed CDN build compatibility with j\+Query and other tools that expose {\ttfamily \$} by properly wrapping the code in an IIFE.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9325}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+6.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/03-\/18}{v3.\+6.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/03-\/18}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9325}

Kudos to @kossnocorp and @fturmel for working on the release.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9334}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9334}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed DST issue in {\ttfamily get\+Overlapping\+Days\+In\+Intervals}, resulting in an inconsistent number of days returned for intervals starting and ending in different DST periods.
\item Fixed functions incorrectly using {\ttfamily trunc} instead of {\ttfamily round}. The bug was introduced in v3.\+3.\+0. The affected functions\+: {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Calendar\+Days}, {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Calendar\+ISOWeeks}, {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Calendar\+Weeks}, {\ttfamily get\+ISOWeek}, {\ttfamily get\+Week}, and {\ttfamily get\+ISOWeeks\+In\+Year}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9335}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+3.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/01-\/20}{v3.\+3.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/01-\/20}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9335}
On this release worked @kossnocorp, @\+The\+Kvikk, @fturmel and @ckcherry23.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9336}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9336}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed the bug in {\ttfamily get\+Overlapping\+Days\+In\+Intervals} caused by incorrect sorting of interval components that led to 0 for timestamps of different lengths.
\item Fixed bugs when working with negative numbers caused by using {\ttfamily Math.\+floor} ({\ttfamily -\/1.\+1} → {\ttfamily -\/2}) instead of {\ttfamily Math.\+trunc} ({\ttfamily -\/1.\+1} → {\ttfamily -\/1}). Most of the conversion functions (i.\+e., {\ttfamily hours\+To\+Minutes}) were affected when passing some negative fractional input. Also, some other functions that could be possibly affected by unfortunate timezone/date combinations were fixed.

The functions that were affected\+: {\ttfamily format}, {\ttfamily parse}, {\ttfamily get\+Unix\+Time}, {\ttfamily days\+To\+Weeks}, {\ttfamily hours\+To\+Milliseconds}, {\ttfamily hours\+To\+Minutes}, {\ttfamily hours\+To\+Seconds}, {\ttfamily milliseconds}, {\ttfamily minutes\+To\+Milliseconds}, {\ttfamily milliseconds\+To\+Minutes}, {\ttfamily months\+To\+Years}, {\ttfamily milliseconds\+To\+Hours}, {\ttfamily milliseconds\+To\+Seconds}, {\ttfamily minutes\+To\+Hours}, {\ttfamily minutes\+To\+Seconds}, {\ttfamily years\+To\+Quarters}, {\ttfamily years\+To\+Months}, {\ttfamily years\+To\+Days}, {\ttfamily weeks\+To\+Days}, {\ttfamily seconds\+To\+Minutes}, {\ttfamily seconds\+To\+Hours}, {\ttfamily quarters\+To\+Years}, {\ttfamily quarters\+To\+Months} and {\ttfamily months\+To\+Quarters}.
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/3269}{\texttt{ Fixed the Czech locale\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily format\+Distance} to include {\ttfamily 1} in {\ttfamily format\+Distance}.}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Seconds} and other functions relying on rounding options that can produce a negative 0.
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/3662}{\texttt{ Added a preprocessor to the locales API, enabling fixing a long-\/standing bug in the French locale.}} (\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/1391}{\texttt{ \#1391}})
\item Added missing {\ttfamily years\+To\+Days} to the FP submodule.
\item Made functions using rounding methods always return {\ttfamily 0} instead of {\ttfamily -\/0}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9337}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9337}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/3653}{\texttt{ Added {\ttfamily format} alias {\ttfamily format\+Date} with corresponding {\ttfamily Format\+Date\+Options} interface}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9338}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+2.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/01-\/09}{v3.\+2.\+0 -\/ 2024-\/01-\/09}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9338}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/3626}{\texttt{ Fixed internal {\ttfamily to\+Date} not processing string arguments properly}}

This release is brought to you by @kossnocorp.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9349}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9349}

\item Fixed is\+Within\+Interval bug caused by incorrectly sorting dates (\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/3623}{\texttt{ \#3623}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9350}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+0.\+3 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/21}{v3.\+0.\+3 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/21}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9350}
\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9351}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9351}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rolled back pointing ESM types to the same {\ttfamily d.\+ts} files. Instead now it copies the content to avoid \href{https://github.com/arethetypeswrong/arethetypeswrong.github.io/blob/main/docs/problems/FalseCJS.md}{\texttt{ the Masquerading as CJS problem}} reported by "{}\+Are the types wrong?"{}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9352}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+0.\+2 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/21}{v3.\+0.\+2 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/21}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9352}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9354}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+0.\+1 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/20}{v3.\+0.\+1 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/20}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9354}
\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9355}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9355}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/3618}{\texttt{ Fixed an error}} in certain environments caused by {\ttfamily d.\+mts} files exporting only types.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9356}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v3.\+0.\+0 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/18}{v3.\+0.\+0 -\/ 2023-\/12-\/18}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9356}
\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9357}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9357}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: date-\/fns is now a dual-\/package with the support of both ESM and Common\+JS. The files exports are now explicitly in the {\ttfamily package.\+json}. The ESM files now have {\ttfamily .mjs} extension.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: The package now has a flat structure, meaning functions are now named {\ttfamily node\+\_\+modules/date-\/fns/add.\+mjs}, locales are {\ttfamily node\+\_\+modules/date-\/fns/locale/en\+US.\+mjs}, etc.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Now all file content’s exported via named exports instead of {\ttfamily export default}, which will require change direct imports i.\+e. {\ttfamily const add\+Days = require(‘date-\/fns/add\+Days’)} to {\ttfamily const \{ add\+Days \} = require(‘date-\/fns/add\+Days’)}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Type\+Script types are now completely rewritten, check out the {\ttfamily d.\+ts} files for more information.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily constants} now is not exported via the index, so to import one use {\ttfamily import \{ days\+In\+Year \} from "{}date-\/fns/constants"{};}. It improves compatibility with setups that modularize imports \href{https://twitter.com/kossnocorp/status/1731181274579325260}{\texttt{ like Next.\+js}}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Functions now don’t check the number of passed arguments, delegating this task to type checkers. The functions are now slimmer because of this.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}} The arguments are not explicitly converted to the target types. Instead, they are passed as is, delegating this task to type checkers.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Functions that accept {\ttfamily Interval} arguments now do not throw an error if the start is before the end and handle it as a negative interval. If one of the properties in an {\ttfamily Invalid Date}, these functions also do not throw and handle them as invalid intervals.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily are\+Intervals\+Overlapping} normalize intervals before comparison, so {\ttfamily \{ start\+: a, end\+: b \}} is practically equivalent to {\ttfamily \{ start\+: b, end\+: a \}}. When comparing intervals with one of the properties being {\ttfamily Invalid Date}, the function will return false unless the others are valid and equal, given the {\ttfamily inclusive} option is passed. Otherwise, and when even one of the intervals has both properties invalid, the function will always return {\ttfamily false}.
\item {\ttfamily get\+Overlapping\+Days\+In\+Intervals} now normalizes intervals before comparison, so {\ttfamily \{ start\+: a, end\+: b \}} is practically equivalent to {\ttfamily \{ start\+: b, end\+: a \}}. If any of the intervals’ properties is an {\ttfamily Invalid Date}, the function will always return 0.
\item {\ttfamily is\+Within\+Interval} now normalizes intervals before comparison, so {\ttfamily \{ start\+: a, end\+: b \}} is practically equivalent to {\ttfamily \{ start\+: b, end\+: a \}}. If any of the intervals’ properties is an {\ttfamily Invalid Date}, the function will always return false.
\item {\ttfamily interval\+To\+Duration} now returns negative durations for negative intervals. If one or both of the interval properties are invalid, the function will return an empty object.
\item The each\+XOf\+Interval functions ({\ttfamily each\+Day\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Hour\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Minute\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Month\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Weekend\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Weekend\+Of\+Month}, {\ttfamily each\+Weekend\+Of\+Year}, {\ttfamily each\+Week\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Year\+Of\+Interval}) now return a reversed array if the passed interval’s start is after the end. Invalid properties will result in an empty array. Functions that accept the {\ttfamily step} option now also allow negative, 0, and NaN values and return reversed results if the step is negative and an empty array otherwise.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily interval\+To\+Duration} now skips 0 values in the resulting duration, resulting in more compact objects with only relevant properties.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily round\+To\+Nearest\+Minutes} now returns {\ttfamily Invalid Date} instead of throwing an error when {\ttfamily nearest\+To} option is less than 1 or more than 30.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: IE is no longer supported.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Now all functions use {\ttfamily Math.\+trunc} rounding method where rounding is required. The behavior is configurable on a per-\/function basis.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Undocumented {\ttfamily only\+Numeric} option was removed from {\ttfamily nn} and {\ttfamily sv} locales. If you relied on it, \href{mailto:koss@nocorp.me}{\texttt{ please contact me}}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: Flow is not supported anymore. If you relied on it, \href{mailto:koss@nocorp.me}{\texttt{ please contact me}}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: The locales now use regular functions instead of the UTC version, which should not break any code unless you used locales directly.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9358}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9358}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All functions that accept date arguments now also accept strings.
\item All functions now export options interfaces.
\item Now functions allow passing custom Date extensions like \href{https://github.com/date-fns/utc}{\texttt{ UTCDate}}. They will detect and use the arguments constructor to generate the result of the same class.
\item {\ttfamily each\+Month\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Quarter\+Of\+Interval}, {\ttfamily each\+Week\+Of\+Interval}, and {\ttfamily each\+Year\+Of\+Interval} now accept the {\ttfamily step} option like most of the each\+XOf\+Interval functions.
\item A new {\ttfamily interval} function that validates interval, emulating the v2 interval functions behavior.
\item {\ttfamily difference\+InX} functions now accept options and allow setting up {\ttfamily rounding\+Method} that configures how the result is rounded. {\ttfamily Math.\+trunc} is the default method.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9359}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v2.\+30.\+0}{v2.\+30.\+0}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9359}
Kudos to @kossnocorp and @\+Andarist for working on the release.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9360}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changes}{Changes}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9360}

\item Fixed increased build size after enabling compatibility with older browsers in the previous release. This was done by adding @babel/runtime as a dependency. \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/3208\#issuecomment-1528592465}{\texttt{ See more details}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9361}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{v2.\+29.\+3 -\/ 2022-\/09-\/13}{v2.\+29.\+3 -\/ 2022-\/09-\/13}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9361}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9484}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/compare/v2.0.0...v2.0.1}{\texttt{ 2.\+0.\+1}} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/23}{\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/compare/v2.0.0...v2.0.1}{\texttt{ 2.\+0.\+1}} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/23}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9484}
\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9485}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9485}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/1046}{\texttt{ Fix}} {\ttfamily get\+Week\+Of\+Month} with {\ttfamily options.\+week\+Starts\+On} set to 1 \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/1040}{\texttt{ not working for Sundays}}. Kudos to \href{https://github.com/waseemahmad31}{\texttt{ @waseemahmad31}}!
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9486}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/compare/v1.28.5...v2.0.0}{\texttt{ 2.\+0.\+0}} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/20}{\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/compare/v1.28.5...v2.0.0}{\texttt{ 2.\+0.\+0}} -\/ 2019-\/08-\/20}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9486}
If you\textquotesingle{}re upgrading from v2 alpha or beta, \href{https://gist.github.com/kossnocorp/a307a464760b405bb78ef5020a4ab136}{\texttt{ see the pre-\/release changelog}}.\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9487}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9487}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed the {\ttfamily to\+Date} bug occurring when parsing ISO-\/8601 style dates (but not valid ISO format) with a trailing Z (e.\+g {\ttfamily 2012-\/01Z}), it returned Invalid Date for Fire\+Fox/\+IE11 \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issue/510}{\texttt{ \#510}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily difference\+In...} functions returning negative zero in some cases\+: \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/692}{\texttt{ \#692}}
\item {\ttfamily is\+Date} now works properly with dates passed across iframes \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/754}{\texttt{ \#754}}.
\item Fixed a few bugs that appeared in timezones with offsets that include seconds (e.\+g. GMT+00\+:57\+:44). See PR \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/789}{\texttt{ \#789}}.
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/1003}{\texttt{ Fixed DST issue}}. See \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/972}{\texttt{ \#972}} and \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/992}{\texttt{ \#992}} for more details.
\item Fixed DST issue in {\ttfamily each\+Day\+Of\+Interval} that caused time in the days after DST change to have the shift as well.
\item Fixed bug in Galician locale caused by incorrect usage of {\ttfamily get\+Hours} instead of {\ttfamily get\+UTCHours}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9488}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9488}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: now functions don\textquotesingle{}t accept string arguments, but only numbers or dates. When a string is passed, it will result in an unexpected result ({\ttfamily Invalid Date}, {\ttfamily NaN}, etc).

From now on a string should be parsed using {\ttfamily parse\+ISO} (ISO 8601) or {\ttfamily parse}.

In v1 we\textquotesingle{}ve used {\ttfamily new Date()} to parse strings, but it resulted in many hard-\/to-\/track bugs caused by inconsistencies in different browsers. To address that we\textquotesingle{}ve implemented our ISO 8601 parser but that made library to significantly grow in size. To prevent inevitable bugs and keep the library tiny, we made this trade-\/off.

See \href{https://blog.date-fns.org/post/we-cut-date-fns-v2-minimal-build-size-down-to-300-bytes-and-now-its-the-smallest-date-library-18f2nvh2z0yal}{\texttt{ this post}} for more details.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v2.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{addDays("{}2016-\/01-\/01"{},\ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v2.0.0\ onward}
\DoxyCodeLine{addDays(parseISO("{}2016-\/01-\/01"{}),\ 1);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: new format string API for {\ttfamily format} function which is based on \href{https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-dates.html\#Date_Field_Symbol_Table}{\texttt{ Unicode Technical Standard \#35}}. See \href{https://blog.date-fns.org/post/unicode-tokens-in-date-fns-v2-sreatyki91jg}{\texttt{ this post}} for more details.
\end{DoxyItemize}

&PPPppp   &&May 29th, 1453 at ...    \\\cline{1-4}
&PPPPpppp   &&Sunday, May 29th, 1453 at ...   \\\cline{1-4}
\end{longtabu}


Characters are now escaped using single quote symbols (`'{\ttfamily ) instead of square brackets. }format\`{} now throws Range\+Error if it encounters an unescaped latin character that isn\textquotesingle{}t a valid formatting token.

To use {\ttfamily YY} and {\ttfamily YYYY} tokens that represent week-\/numbering years, you should set {\ttfamily use\+Additional\+Week\+Year\+Tokens} option\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{format(Date.now(),\ "{}YY"{},\ \{\ useAdditionalWeekYearTokens:\ true\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//=>\ '86'}

\end{DoxyCode}


To use {\ttfamily D} and {\ttfamily DD} tokens which represent days of the year, set {\ttfamily use\+Additional\+Day\+Of\+Year\+Tokens} option\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{format(Date.now(),\ "{}D"{},\ \{\ useAdditionalDayOfYearTokens:\ true\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//=>\ '364'}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: function submodules now use camel\+Case naming schema\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v2.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ differenceInCalendarISOYears\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/difference\_in\_calendar\_iso\_years"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v2.0.0\ onward}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ differenceInCalendarISOYears\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/differenceInCalendarISOYears"{};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: min and max functions now accept an array of dates rather than spread arguments.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v2.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ date1\ =\ new\ Date(1989,\ 6\ /*\ Jul\ */,\ 10);}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ date2\ =\ new\ Date(1987,\ 1\ /*\ Feb\ */,\ 11);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ minDate\ =\ min(date1,\ date2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ maxDate\ =\ max(date1,\ date2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v2.0.0\ onward:}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ dates\ =\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(1989,\ 6\ /*\ Jul\ */,\ 10),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(1987,\ 1\ /*\ Feb\ */,\ 11),}
\DoxyCodeLine{];}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ minDate\ =\ min(dates);}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ maxDate\ =\ max(dates);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: make the second argument of {\ttfamily format} required for the sake of explicitness.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v2.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{format(new\ Date(2016,\ 0,\ 1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v2.0.0\ onward}
\DoxyCodeLine{format(new\ Date(2016,\ 0,\ 1),\ "{}yyyy-\/MM-\/dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSSxxx"{});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}} renamed ISO week-\/numbering year helpers\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily add\+ISOYears} → {\ttfamily add\+ISOWeek\+Years}
\item {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Calendar\+ISOYears} → {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Calendar\+ISOWeek\+Years}
\item {\ttfamily difference\+In\+ISOYears} → {\ttfamily difference\+In\+ISOWeek\+Years}
\item {\ttfamily end\+Of\+ISOYear} → {\ttfamily end\+Of\+ISOWeek\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily get\+ISOYear} → {\ttfamily get\+ISOWeek\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily is\+Same\+ISOYear} → {\ttfamily is\+Same\+ISOWeek\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily last\+Day\+Of\+ISOYear} → {\ttfamily last\+Day\+Of\+ISOWeek\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily set\+ISOYear} → {\ttfamily set\+ISOWeek\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily sub\+ISOYears} → {\ttfamily sub\+ISOWeek\+Years}
\end{DoxyItemize}

i.\+e. "{}\+ISO year"{} renamed to "{}\+ISO week year"{}, which is short for \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_week_date}{\texttt{ ISO week-\/numbering year}}. It makes them consistent with locale-\/dependent week-\/numbering year helpers, e.\+g., {\ttfamily start\+Of\+Week\+Year}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: functions renamed\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily are\+Ranges\+Overlapping} → {\ttfamily are\+Intervals\+Overlapping}
\item {\ttfamily each\+Day} → {\ttfamily each\+Day\+Of\+Interval}
\item {\ttfamily get\+Overlapping\+Days\+In\+Ranges} → {\ttfamily get\+Overlapping\+Days\+In\+Intervals}
\item {\ttfamily is\+Within\+Range} → {\ttfamily is\+Within\+Interval}
\end{DoxyItemize}

This change was made to mirror the use of the word "{}interval"{} in standard ISO 8601\+:2004 terminology\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2.1.3}
\DoxyCodeLine{time\ interval}
\DoxyCodeLine{part\ of\ the\ time\ axis\ limited\ by\ two\ instants}

\end{DoxyCode}


Also these functions now accept an object with {\ttfamily start} and {\ttfamily end} properties instead of two arguments as an interval. All these functions throw {\ttfamily Range\+Error} if the start of the interval is after its end or if any date in the interval is {\ttfamily Invalid Date}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v2.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{areRangesOverlapping(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 10),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 20),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 17),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 21),}
\DoxyCodeLine{);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{eachDay(new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 10),\ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 20));}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{getOverlappingDaysInRanges(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 10),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 20),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 17),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 21),}
\DoxyCodeLine{);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{isWithinRange(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 3),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 1),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2014,\ 0,\ 7),}
\DoxyCodeLine{);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v2.0.0\ onward}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: functions renamed\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words} → {\ttfamily format\+Distance}
\item {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words\+Strict} → {\ttfamily format\+Distance\+Strict}
\item {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words\+To\+Now} → {\ttfamily format\+Distance\+To\+Now}
\end{DoxyItemize}

to make them consistent with {\ttfamily format} and {\ttfamily format\+Relative}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: The order of arguments of {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words} and {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words\+Strict} is swapped to make them consistent with {\ttfamily difference\+In...} functions.

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily partial\+Method} option in {\ttfamily format\+Distance\+Strict} is renamed to {\ttfamily rounding\+Method}.

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: in {\ttfamily format\+Distance\+Strict}, if {\ttfamily rounding\+Method} is not specified, it now defaults to {\ttfamily round} instead of {\ttfamily floor}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily unit} option in {\ttfamily format\+Distance\+Strict} now accepts one of the strings\+: \textquotesingle{}second\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}minute\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}hour\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}day\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}month\textquotesingle{} or \textquotesingle{}year\textquotesingle{} instead of \textquotesingle{}s\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}m\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}d\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}M\textquotesingle{} or \textquotesingle{}Y\textquotesingle{}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily parse} that previously used to convert strings and numbers to dates now parses only strings in an arbitrary format specified as an argument. Use {\ttfamily to\+Date} to coerce numbers and {\ttfamily parse\+ISO} to parse ISO 8601 strings.

\DoxyCodeLine{toDate(1547005581366);}
\DoxyCodeLine{toDate(new\ Date());\ //\ Clone\ the\ date}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily to\+Date} (previously {\ttfamily parse}) now doesn\textquotesingle{}t accept string arguments but only numbers and dates. {\ttfamily to\+Date} called with an invalid argument will return {\ttfamily Invalid Date}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: new locale format. See \href{https://date-fns.org/docs/Locale}{\texttt{ docs/\+Locale}}. Locales renamed\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily en} → {\ttfamily en-\/\+US}
\item {\ttfamily zh\+\_\+cn} → {\ttfamily zh-\/\+CN}
\item {\ttfamily zh\+\_\+tw} → {\ttfamily zh-\/\+TW}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: now {\ttfamily closest\+To} and {\ttfamily closest\+Index\+To} don\textquotesingle{}t throw an exception when the second argument is not an array, and return Invalid Date instead.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: now {\ttfamily is\+Valid} doesn\textquotesingle{}t throw an exception if the first argument is not an instance of Date. Instead, argument is converted beforehand using {\ttfamily to\+Date}.

class="{}markdown\+Table\+Body\+None"{}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}Type\+Error{\ttfamily \textbackslash{}ilinebr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/td\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}td class="{}markdown\+Table\+Body\+None"{}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}false\`{}   \\\cline{1-3}
\end{longtabu}


We introduce this change to make {\itshape date-\/fns} consistent with ECMAScript behavior that try to coerce arguments to the expected type (which is also the case with other {\itshape date-\/fns} functions).


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: functions now throw {\ttfamily Range\+Error} if optional values passed to {\ttfamily options} are not {\ttfamily undefined} or have expected values. This change is introduced for consistency with ECMAScript standard library which does the same.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily format}, {\ttfamily format\+Distance} (previously {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words}) and {\ttfamily format\+Distance\+Strict} (previously {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words\+Strict}) now throw {\ttfamily Range\+Error} if one of the passed arguments is invalid. It reflects behavior of {\ttfamily to\+ISOString} and Intl API. See \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/1032}{\texttt{ \#1032}}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: all functions now implicitly convert arguments by following rules\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}

\tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{5}{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ date   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ number   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ string   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ boolean    }\\\cline{1-5}
\endfirsthead
\hline
\endfoot
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ date   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ number   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ string   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ boolean    }\\\cline{1-5}
\endhead
0   &new Date(0)   &0   &\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{}   &false    \\\cline{1-5}
\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{}   &Invalid Date   &0   &\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{}   &false    \\\cline{1-5}
1   &new Date(1)   &1   &\textquotesingle{}1\textquotesingle{}   &true    \\\cline{1-5}
\textquotesingle{}1\textquotesingle{}   &Invalid Date   &1   &\textquotesingle{}1\textquotesingle{}   &true    \\\cline{1-5}
true   &Invalid Date   &NaN   &\textquotesingle{}true\textquotesingle{}   &true    \\\cline{1-5}
false   &Invalid Date   &NaN   &\textquotesingle{}false\textquotesingle{}   &false    \\\cline{1-5}
null   &Invalid Date   &NaN   &\textquotesingle{}null\textquotesingle{}   &false    \\\cline{1-5}
undefined   &Invalid Date   &NaN   &\textquotesingle{}undefined\textquotesingle{}   &false    \\\cline{1-5}
NaN   &Invalid Date   &NaN   &\textquotesingle{}NaN\textquotesingle{}   &false   \\\cline{1-5}
\end{longtabu}


Notes\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item as before, arguments expected to be {\ttfamily Date} are converted to {\ttfamily Date} using {\itshape date-\/fns\textquotesingle{}} {\ttfamily to\+Date} function;
\item arguments expected to be numbers are converted to integer numbers using our custom {\ttfamily to\+Integer} implementation (see \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/765}{\texttt{ \#765}});
\item arguments expected to be strings are converted to strings using Java\+Script\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily String} function;
\item arguments expected to be booleans are converted to boolean using Java\+Script\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Boolean} function.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily null} and {\ttfamily undefined} passed to optional arguments (i.\+e. properties of {\ttfamily options} argument) are ignored as if no argument was passed.

If any resulting argument is invalid (i.\+e. {\ttfamily NaN} for numbers and {\ttfamily Invalid Date} for dates), an invalid value will be returned\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily false} for functions that return booleans (expect {\ttfamily is\+Valid});
\item {\ttfamily Invalid Date} for functions that return dates;
\item and {\ttfamily NaN} for functions that return numbers.
\end{DoxyItemize}

See tests and PRs \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/460}{\texttt{ \#460}} and \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/765}{\texttt{ \#765}} for exact behavior.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: all functions now check if the passed number of arguments is less than the number of required arguments and will throw {\ttfamily Type\+Error} exception if so.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: all functions that accept numbers as arguments, now coerce values using {\ttfamily Number()} and also round off decimals. Positive decimals are rounded using {\ttfamily Math.\+floor}, decimals less than zero are rounded using {\ttfamily Math.\+ceil}.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: The Bower \& UMD/\+CDN package versions are no longer supported.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily null} now is not a valid date. {\ttfamily is\+Valid(null)} returns {\ttfamily false}; {\ttfamily to\+Date(null)} returns an invalid date. Since {\ttfamily to\+Date} is used internally by all the functions, operations over {\ttfamily null} will also return an invalid date. \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/issues/537}{\texttt{ See \#537}} for the reasoning.
\item {\ttfamily to\+Date} (previously {\ttfamily parse}) and {\ttfamily is\+Valid} functions now accept {\ttfamily any} type as the first argument.
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/837}{\texttt{ Exclude {\ttfamily docs.\+json} from the npm package}}. Kudos to \href{https://github.com/hawkrives}{\texttt{ @hawkrives}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9489}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9489}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item FP functions like those in \href{https://github.com/lodash/lodash/wiki/FP-Guide}{\texttt{ lodash}}, that support \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Currying}{\texttt{ currying}}, and, as a consequence, functional-\/style \href{https://medium.com/making-internets/why-using-chain-is-a-mistake-9bc1f80d51ba}{\texttt{ function composing}}.

Functions with options ({\ttfamily format}, {\ttfamily parse}, etc.) have two FP counterparts\+: one that has the options object as its first argument and one that hasn\textquotesingle{}t. The name of the former has {\ttfamily With\+Options} added to the end of its name.

In FP functions, the order of arguments is reversed.

See \href{https://date-fns.org/docs/FP-Guide}{\texttt{ FP Guide}} for more information.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ addYears\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/fp/addYears"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ formatWithOptions\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/fp/formatWithOptions"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ eo\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/locale/eo"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ If\ FP\ function\ has\ not\ received\ enough\ arguments,\ it\ returns\ another\ function}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ addFiveYears\ =\ addYears(5);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Several\ arguments\ can\ be\ curried\ at\ once}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ dateToString\ =\ formatWithOptions(\{\ locale:\ eo\ \},\ "{}d\ MMMM\ yyyy"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ dates\ =\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2017,\ 0\ /*\ Jan\ */,\ 1),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2017,\ 1\ /*\ Feb\ */,\ 11),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ new\ Date(2017,\ 6\ /*\ Jul\ */,\ 2),}
\DoxyCodeLine{];}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ formattedDates\ =\ dates.map((date)\ =>\ dateToString(addFiveYears(date)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{//=>\ ['1\ januaro\ 2022',\ '11\ februaro\ 2022',\ '2\ julio\ 2022']}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Added support for \href{http://www.ecma-international.org/ecma-262/6.0/\#sec-modules}{\texttt{ ECMAScript Modules}}.

It allows usage with bundlers that support tree-\/shaking, like \href{http://rollupjs.org}{\texttt{ rollup.\+js}} and \href{https://webpack.js.org}{\texttt{ webpack}}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Without\ tree-\/shaking:}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ format\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/format"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ parse\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/parse"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ With\ tree-\/shaking:}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ format,\ parse\ \}\ from\ "{}date-\/fns"{};}

\end{DoxyCode}


Also, ESM functions provide default export, they can be used with Type\+Script to import functions in more idiomatic way\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ *\ as\ format\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/format"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Now}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ format\ from\ "{}date-\/fns/format"{};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily format\+Relative} function. See \href{https://date-fns.org/docs/formatRelative}{\texttt{ format\+Relative}}
\item Flow typings for {\ttfamily index.\+js}, {\ttfamily fp/index.\+js}, {\ttfamily locale/index.\+js}, and their ESM equivalents. See PR \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/558}{\texttt{ \#558}}
\item New locale-\/dependent week-\/numbering year helpers\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily get\+Week}
\item {\ttfamily get\+Week\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily set\+Week}
\item {\ttfamily set\+Week\+Year}
\item {\ttfamily start\+Of\+Week\+Year}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily each\+Week\+Of\+Interval}, the weekly equivalent of {\ttfamily each\+Day\+Of\+Interval}
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/870}{\texttt{ Added {\ttfamily get\+Unix\+Time} function}}. Kudos to \href{https://github.com/Kingwl}{\texttt{ @\+Kingwl}}.
\item \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/839}{\texttt{ New decade helpers}}. Thanks to \href{https://github.com/y-nk}{\texttt{ @y-\/nk}}!
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily get\+Decade}
\item {\ttfamily start\+Of\+Decade}
\item {\ttfamily end\+Of\+Decade}
\item {\ttfamily last\+Day\+Of\+Decade}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words}, {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words\+To\+Now}, {\ttfamily distance\+In\+Words\+Strict} and {\ttfamily format} functions now check if the passed locale is valid, and fallback to English locale otherwise. See PR\+: \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/321}{\texttt{ \#321}}
\item {\itshape Internal}\+: use a loop instead of {\ttfamily Object.\+keys} in {\ttfamily build\+Formatting\+Tokens\+Reg\+Exp} to improve compatibility with older browsers. See PR\+: \href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/pull/322}{\texttt{ \#322}}

\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9570}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9570}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily parse} now can parse dates that are ISO 8601 centuries (e.\+g., {\ttfamily 19} and {\ttfamily +0019}).


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ result\ =\ parse("{}19"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//=>\ Mon\ Jan\ 01\ 1900\ 00:00:00}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item In {\ttfamily parse}, added ability to specify the number of additional digits for extended year or century format (possible values are 0, 1 or 2; default is 2).


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{parse("{}+002016-\/11-\/01"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{parse("{}+02016-\/11-\/01"{},\ \{\ additionalDigits:\ 1\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{parse("{}+2016-\/11-\/01"{},\ \{\ additionalDigits:\ 0\ \});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9571}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/compare/v1.8.1...v1.9.0}{\texttt{ 1.\+9.\+0}} -\/ 2016-\/10-\/25}{\href{https://github.com/date-fns/date-fns/compare/v1.8.1...v1.9.0}{\texttt{ 1.\+9.\+0}} -\/ 2016-\/10-\/25}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9571}

\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9599}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9599}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily format} now returns the correct result for key {\ttfamily E}.
\item Prevent {\ttfamily start\+Of...}, {\ttfamily end\+Of...} and {\ttfamily last\+Day\+Of...} functions to return dates with an incorrect time when the date is modifying into another time zone.
\item {\ttfamily parse} now parses years from 1 AD to 99 AD correctly.
\item Fix a bug in {\ttfamily get\+ISOWeek} appearing because of a changing time zone (e.\+g., when the given date is in DST and the start of the ISO year is not).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9600}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9600}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: all functions are moved to the root of the library, so they are now accessible with `require(\textquotesingle{}date-\/fns/name\+\_\+of\+\_\+function'){\ttfamily or }import name\+Of\+Function from \textquotesingle{}date-\/fns/name\+\_\+of\+\_\+function\textquotesingle{}\`{}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v1.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ addMonths\ =\ require("{}date-\/fns/src/add\_months"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v1.0.0\ onward}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ addMonths\ =\ require("{}date-\/fns/add\_months"{});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: functions that had the last optional argument {\ttfamily week\+Starts\+At} (i.\+e. {\ttfamily end\+Of\+Week}, {\ttfamily is\+Same\+Week}, {\ttfamily last\+Day\+Of\+Week}, {\ttfamily set\+Day}, {\ttfamily start\+Of\+Week}) now instead receive the object {\ttfamily options} with the property {\ttfamily options.\+week\+Starts\+On} as the last argument.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Before\ v1.0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ result\ =\ endOfWeek(new\ Date(2014,\ 8,\ 2),\ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ v1.0.0\ onward}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ result\ =\ endOfWeek(new\ Date(2014,\ 8,\ 2),\ \{\ weekStartsOn:\ 1\ \});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: remove the function {\ttfamily get\+Time\+Since\+Midnight} that was used inside the other functions.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily difference\+In\+Days} now returns the number of full days instead of calendar days.
\item {\bfseries{BREAKING}}\+: {\ttfamily each\+Day} and {\ttfamily is\+Within\+Range} now throw an exception when the given range boundaries are invalid.
\item Faster {\ttfamily is\+Leap\+Year}.
\item {\itshape Internal}\+: make the documentation more verbose.
\item {\itshape Internal}\+: convert the tests from Chai to power-\/assert allowing them to run against IE8.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9601}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md__2home_2solype_2delivery_2current__days_2trello_2front_2node__modules_2date-fns_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md9601}
